icon-linegraph\"></i><h5>Data Driven Culture Made Easy</h5><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">SchoolStatus delivers all of your instructional data through beautiful, intuitive visualizations. SchoolStatus allows for fast reporting like you've never seen.</p></div></div></div></div></section><a href=\"#\" id=\"welcome\" class=\"in-page-link\"></a><section class=\"side-image text-heavy clearfix dark-wrapper\"><div class=\"image-container col-md-5 col-sm-3 pull-left\"><div class=\"background-image-holder\" style=\"background: url(&quot;https://cdn.schoolstatus.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/what-we-do.png?x46101&quot;) 50% 0%;\"> <img class=\"background-image\" alt=\"Background Image\" src=\"https://cdn.schoolstatus.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/what-we-do.png?x46101\" pagespeed_url_hash=\"2685508496\" style=\"display: none;\"></div></div><div class=\"container\"><div class=\"row\"><div class=\"col-md-6 col-md-offset-6 col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-4 content clearfix\"><div class=\"row\"><div id=\"aq-block-142-9\" class=\"aq-block aq-block-aq_section_title_block col-sm-12 aq-first aq-last \"><div class=\"\"><h1 class=\"\">Moving instructional data and analysis into a new era of change.</h1></div><div class=\"lead  \"><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">At this point, most school districts are collecting and tracking data in some form or fashion. But rather than leave it on a 'data warehouse' shelf to collect dust, SchoolStatus presents your data in a way that highlights the information most valuable to your team, and can actually be used to impact instruction on a day-to-day basis.&nbsp;</p><p><a href=\"/about\" class=\"btn btn-primary\" target=\"_self\">Learn More</a></p></div></div><div id=\"aq-block-142-10\" class=\"aq-block aq-block-aq_ebor_text_block col-sm-6 aq-first \"><div class=\"feature\"><h5>Parent Collaboration</h5><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Through our mobile parent portal StudentStatus, parents and teachers can discuss mutually-available information in real time via in-app messaging. Bridging this gap between home and school provides students with a data-driven support system focused on success.</p></div></div><div id=\"aq-block-142-11\" class=\"aq-block aq-block-aq_ebor_text_block col-sm-6  aq-last \"><div class=\"feature\"><h5>Included PD &amp; Training</h5><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">We believe supporting our customers should be our first priority. Through 24/7 in-house phone support, live chat, and unlimited on-site training, SchoolStatus lives out our customer-centric approach to service.&nbsp;We're here with you and your team every step of the way.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></section><a href=\"#\" id=\"demo-video\" class=\"in-page-link\"></a><section class=\"aq-block light-wrapper\"><div class=\"container\"><div class=\"row\"><div id=\"aq-block-142-13\" class=\"aq-block aq-block-aq_section_title_block col-sm-6 aq-first \"><span class=\" alt-font  ebor-block\">LEARN MORE ABOUT WHAT MAKES US DIFFERENT</span><div class=\"\"><h1 class=\"\"></h1><h1 style=\"font-size: 2.0em;\">Relevant, actionable, and secure.<br>This will change education, forever.</h1></div><div class=\"lead  \"><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Get a quick overview of just what makes SchoolStatus so important when it comes to putting your instructional data to use helping students.
